<span style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">          </span>Further, this book is intended
to be a book of peace, love and good will to the entire world, and those
that may misuse it for negative thoughts, emotions and actions,
including, but not limited to: hate, violence, rage, war, anger,
judgment, unhappiness, sadness, fear, despair and anxiety, are herewith
warned that they will experience soul suffering on the day of their
resurrection, and they will feel all the pain, suffering and agony they
caused others.</span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">          </span>Therefore the reader is wished
the following positive thoughts, emotions and actions which are taught
in this good book: love, peace, joy, happiness, forgiveness, helpfulness
towards one another, compassion, empathy, sympathy, hope and
trust.</span>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">          </span>LIMITED LICENSE: It is the
intent of the author to promote peace, love, harmony and goodwill
throughout the world and to that end, this book may be read aloud during
any worship service or during any religious study group; *provided
that*, in no manner may the book be used to promote any negative action
or emotion including, but not limited to: war, hate, death, destruction
or the creation of rage or anxiety in any person or persons.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Please contact
<joanne@mothergoddess.org> if you are interested in rights to reprint or
copy this book in areas of the world which are war torn, and a one year
license to do so will be freely granted.</span>

style="mso-tab-count:1">                              
</span></span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">DEDICATIONS</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>This book is dedicated to my husband, and our four
children who are always very understanding of my long hours and hard
work for them, as well as my mother Jean Marie, and my late father,
Robert William.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>I am especially
grateful to my mother’s assistance in editing this work, and her
appreciation for it. I am also highly appreciative to Sylvia Browne,
Edgar Cayce, James Twyman, Doreen Virtue and Helen Schucman (*A Course
in Miracles)* for their work channeling information from the other side
so that we know the Divine is only peace and love. <span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>And finally, I do not believe that I
would have set upon this path of feminine sacred writing without the
very special assistance from my own 10 year old daughter, who is an
indigo child, and who started chattering away about peace, love and
Mother Goddess, Father God, angels and fairies from her very first words
as a toddler.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>I would like to
thank all of these very special people, as well as my many friends that
believe in peace, love and the angels as well.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>It is also dedicated to all the women and girls
around the world that are discriminated against in more ways that are
shameful for any good person to imagine.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Please visit [www.RAWA.org<span style="mso-footnote-id:ftn1"
title=""><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span
style="mso-special-character:
footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><u><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
color:blue;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:
AR-SA">\[1\]</span></u></span></span></span></span>](https://www.RAWA.org)
to see but a few examples. Treaties are ignored, medical funding for
poor pregnant women and infants is often withheld, all because it is
considered to be culturally acceptable to do so.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">   </span>Female genital mutilation, denial of
access to books, career opportunities and education are nothing but a
form of forced slavery.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>This must
end.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>This book is further
dedicated to all the women and children who have suffered under such
“rules” and “cultural acceptance” which have amounted to little more
than shameful cruelty and severe oppression of the female gender.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>A portion of the proceeds of every book will to be
sent to charities benefitting poor and oppressed women and girls around
the world, including the U.S.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>I
further hope that some day computers may be sent to every girl and
uneducated or undereducated woman around the world so that they might
receive a good education via the internet.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
4">                                                </span></span>

<span
style="font-size:17.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Lydian Csv BT&quot;">MAY
MOTHER GODDESS BLESS THEM ALL!</span>

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Lydian Csv BT&quot;"></span>

 

<span
style="font-size:15.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Lydian Csv BT&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                        
</span></span><span
style="font-size:24.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;WP IconicSymbolsA&quot;">!!!!!!!!!</span><span
style="font-size:15.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Lydian Csv BT&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:16.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Lydian Csv BT&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:24.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;WP IconicSymbolsA&quot;">‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚</span><span
style="font-size:28.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:28.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span
style="font-size:28.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                          </span></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">FORWARD</span><span
style="font-size:28.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:28.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:28.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">    </span></span><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This book is intended to be
a book of complete love, peace and spirituality.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">   </span>It has eliminates hate and violence
from a most important sacred writing to usher in a new age of
spirituality for an advanced planet and its inhabitants.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>It brings a new path to womankind
towards the Divine and is especially geared toward women and girls.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Concepts of
polygyny<a href="#_ftn2" id="_ftnref2"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[2]</span></span></span></span></a> and
discrimination towards females are herewith dispensed with.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Women should have freedoms equal to
that of men, including the right to delay marriage and the right to an
education up to and including college.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Separation of the sexes is as wrongful as slavery.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The concept of sexual discrimination
as a “cultural matter” is an obvious and severe mistake.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>This is because a man of quality
understands women for equality.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                   
</span>INTRODUCTION TO THE KORANA</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>This book is an entirely new interpretation of the
Koran, and it has been written by a woman entirely for women and
girls.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Did you ever try to read
the Koran only to be grossly disappointed that it was geared almost
exclusively toward men, and in particular, toward a male God?<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Or perhaps you found the use of war as
an acceptable tool to settle differences, make money and spread religion
to be abhorrent?<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>In addition,
much of the original book simply does not make much sense to non-Arab
women that do not know the nuances of Arab culture and traditions. Maybe
you found that the language used in the traditional versions of Shakir,
Abdullah Yusufali and Pickthal use such archaic English that it is near
impossible to read and understand the traditional former English Koran
texts.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>Well, this is your book.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>This Korana version has been almost
exclusively feminized.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Goddess
has been used instead of God.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The
stories refer to women prophetesses and not men.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The heros are heroines--Sarah (wife of
Abraham), Nora (wife of Noah), Wileh (wife of Lot), etc., because they
were in fact high priestesses and prophetesses in and of
themselves.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Many footnotes
explain references specific to ancient Arab culture so you will not have
to continually guess what was being referred to.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The book teaches peace and not
war.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>It teaches hell as an
allegory to the process of reincarnation and earth as a school.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Gabriel is referred to in feminine
form as Gabrielle.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>A table is
given to convert traditional names and places to feminized ones.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The book is not centered on
prohibiting the worship of Goddess via multiple idols and instead it is
more centered on prohibiting the association of negative actions and
emotions with Her, which is far more important.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>In this Korana, Goddess does not maim,
kill, hate, commit acts of vengeance or retribution, nor does she engage
in actions of violence and cursing against any person--She is pure
love.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The traditional Arab
stories are rich and amazing and of interest to everyone.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The concepts of Jesus Christ (Yeshua)
and Mother Mary are especially interesting because they are based upon
Gospels not found in the New Testament, but were in existence in 625 CE
and were believed by many to be true and accurate.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Neither Christian nor Jew should be
offended by any derogatory statements, because these have been made into
positive ones.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>The Book was written in a prose format for two
purposes.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>First, it makes it
easier for people to read the Book aloud during a worship service, and
it also allows the reader to get a sense of the original document where
a few chapters were written in rhyme and meter, but the rest were
written in soft prose.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Alliteration and soft internal rhyming in sentences are kept for
the same purpose.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>If you find anything whatsoever in this book that
promotes hate, violence, aggression, greed, self centeredness, or
anything that shows Goddess in a negative light, please post it on my
website at [www.MotherGoddess.org](https://www.MotherGoddess.org) on the
bulletin board there and it will be promptly revised.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
5">                                                           
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>Note this book was written and inspired by George
Sale’s Koran version which shows a publication date of 1860.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>This book included many footnotes of
detailed explanation of Arab culture and stories.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>It has been compared with the
traditional versions by<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Shakir,
Abdullah Yusufali and Pickthal and others for accuracy.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>This book is copyrighted and may not
be further copied or disseminated without written permission of the
author.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">   </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span></span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Many chapters being with
initials, the meaning of which has long ago been lost.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>To the extent that some meanings have
been found in publications, they are given as suggested ones
here.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Names of
angels and archangels overwhelming female!</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Does it
matter?<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>No.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Sylvia says they don’t really have
individual names anyway!<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>(Her
spirit guide Francine calls them all “Michael”)<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>And since they don’t incarnate, they
really don’t have a true gender as people do.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Ask for an archangel, and if you want
a female, you will get a female!<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>They are assigned according to what you need to have done and
they come prepared.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>If you ask
them their name, they will give it to you, generally based upon whatever
name you think is the best one.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">On
Eblis–the fallen angel.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Legend
has it that Eblis challenged Goddess and was banished from heaven to
mislead womankind and eat unblessed food and haunt ruins.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>However, when Eblis arrived on earth,
he began to foment hot winds which killed many of the people, so the
angelic army went down to capture him and return him to heaven to learn
heavenly ways.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>He learned and
gained much stature there, until he got into trouble again and was
banished back to earth until the day of final judgment when he will be
cleansed.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>He is often synonymous
with “the devil” or “Satan”, both very old evil deities or
semi-deities.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Sylvia
says there are no dark angels because of the way they are created.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>However, dark entities as ghosts
sometimes are afraid to pass over because they think they will go to
hell, or they are attached to something material that they love, such as
a beautiful home or even a self portrait of them in beauty.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>If you happen upon a situation such as
this, it is better to dump the home or item than have a nasty
poltergeist hanging around.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Although they cannot really harm you, they will scare you much as
they can, and they can trip, slap, break and throw things.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
9">                                                                                                           
</span></span>
